1) **Hard Constraints**
- Property must be in the **Burlington area**.
- Budget range: **CAD $650,000 – $750,000**.
- Must be **2-bedroom**, **accessible** (suitable for aging in place), and **low-maintenance** (e.g., condo or bungalow).
- Financing should primarily use **home equity** (cash or partial financing).
- Must include arrangements for **legal services**, **property surveys**, **moving**, and **utility setup**.

2) **Soft Constraints**
- Preference for **quiet neighborhoods**, **proximity to amenities**, or **medical facilities**.
- Preference for **turnkey or recently updated** units to reduce renovation needs.
- Flexibility in **possession date** depending on sale of current home.
- Family coordination and heirloom distribution may be flexible in timing but should be handled sensitively.

3) **Task Decomposition**
   - **Step 1:** Gather user and spouse details (confirm current home equity, ownership, and financial position).
   - **Step 2:** Request children's contact info and check for any recent emails or calendar events related to family discussions.
   - **Step 3:** Ask the external agent (real estate agent) for a list of suitable Burlington properties matching the budget and accessibility criteria.
   - **Step 4:** Obtain financing solutions: determine if full cash purchase from home equity is feasible or if a small bridge loan is needed.
   - **Step 5:** Coordinate with external services:
       - Legal services (real estate lawyer, title transfer, closing costs)
       - Property surveyors (inspection, appraisal)
       - Moving services (quote, packing, transport)
       - Utility/setup services (gas, electricity, internet, change of address)
   - **Step 6:** Calculate total budget breakdown including purchase price, legal, closing, and moving costs.
   - **Step 7:** Plan and draft a family discussion outline about downsizing, including how to approach heirloom distribution. Identify which children should be contacted and possibly set a family Zoom meeting or dinner.

4) **Data Planning (requests to environment)**
   - Request user’s **name** and **spouse’s name**.
   - Request **children’s contact information** and any **recent emails** related to downsizing or family discussions.
   - Request **banking or financial information** on **home equity or available funds**.
   - Check the **calendar** for any upcoming family events or property-related appointments.
   - Possibly retrieve **previous property address** and **ownership details** to estimate equity.

5) **Anticipated Changes**
   - The exact property choice may change depending on availability and price flexibility.
   - Financing method (cash vs. partial mortgage) may shift after reviewing home equity.
   - Moving and legal service providers may vary based on quotes.
   - Family meeting format or timing may adapt based on children’s availability.
